< text>
I meant to write this yesterday, Saturday, after my lovely new bedroom set was delivered and set up on Friday. However sleeping on my new mattress set (closeout from Macy's awesome!) in my wonderful and beautiful new Constellation black bedroom set took up a lot of my time!  The setup was great as Joe did an excellent job despite me sneaking in several times to oh and ah about it and talk his head off.  I ordered this online and unfortunately due to the huge amount of fraud going on in the world today I had to go into the local store and confirm my ID and Credit card. Would love to state that this level of fraud and financial abuse is due to today's problems, that's not true. I worked at Bank of America in the early 1980's when it was only a California bank. Every 6 months we had the newest FBI graduate come in to give us bank tellers the information on the latest frauds usually being perpetrated on the elderly. We bank tellers were the last line of defense before the victim handed over their money to the scam artist. So it behooves all of us to always be careful with our money and for vendors to be sure they are getting their products to a legitimate purchaser.  I really do love the bedroom set and would most definitely purchase more from Oak Furniture in the future. After all there is more of the bedroom set pieces for me to get to round out my remodel and decorating of my master bedroom!</text>

I called Southland AC to schedule service as my unit started to shut off during extreme heat.  After a few questions, Sherry informed me that I was also eligible for a LADWP Nest Thermostat program which was awesome because I had an older thermostat and could use a new wi-fi one.

Their technician, Sev, arrived exactly on time and was very courteous.  He explained to me what he was going to do, asked me a few questions and off he was.  Exactly two hours later, and after spending probably around an hour on the roof in 100 degree heat, he came back saying that it's all done.  He then connected my phone to the new nest wifi unit he just installed.  And, he also fixed a missing wire which was prompting my unit to shut down in extreme heat.  The unit was fully optimized and fixed to work through this season and many more (my unit is about 10 years old and I was worried I"m going to have to get it replaced now).

<user_id>114050157392774228613< /user_id>< review>
I signed up for an annual maintenance contract with Southland Heating and Air. In October 2021 they came for the first visit to our home, ran routine diagnostic tests and changed the filters in our heating system. They also inspected the sophisticated filter we added, Trane's Clean Effects Air Scrubber which uses UV light and other technologies to reduce particles in the air to a tiny number. They did great. Very professional and knowledgable.

Six months later Southland Air took the initiative to call me, without being asked, to schedule their air conditioning maintence technician; I was glad  they reminded me we were due. Their tech Pedro Orellana was courteous, professional, and very skilled; he was even totally familiar with our Air Scubber, and the new HVAC system we have. He let me know the ultraviolet lightbulb in the Clean Effects filter was burned out and needed changing.

The company would have replaced the UV bulb, but I wanted to shop around and instead asked them to email me the part name and number. They did within a day.

GREAT company!! Well-managed, awesome HVAC group. If you're looking for someone to maintain or install your HAVAC system, look no further. This is a seriously well-run company, and the cost of their annual maintenance contract is lower than I found elsewhere, too. Glad we found them!< /review>

So happy with my Southland Heater and Air Conditioner Installation. I had intended to move my air conditioner during a backyard pool building project to make room for an outdoor kitchen.

As it turned out, we discovered that it would be better to replace the unit with a side fan Air Condenser and move it the other side of the house, and replace the furnace with an electric forced air heater. While I did purchase a much more expensive project, I am already seeing the value.

Matt, the co-founder, met with me personally and spent a considerable amount of time helping me understand the options for new HVAC system and whether or not I needed to replace certain things. He did everything he could to help me find an Air Conditioning and Heater / Furnace product that met my needs and my budget.

Matt also connected me with an excellent electrician who set up the new power needs from my box to the attic. "This is the cleanest build I've seen!" was what my pool builder told me.

Working with the entire Southland team was such an easy experience. They were incredibly respectful of my home, laying down tons of plastic and avoiding any damage to my walls, hardwood, or carpet. There was no damage to my stucco, and they sealed and protected everything they had to run electric lines along. I met with the project manager, and he was very proactive in letting me know about the process and what to expect. I had text message and email alerts to help me prepare for the day, as well as milestones afterward including follow up HVAC Service & Installation, and HVAC Inspections by the county.

Today, we have a very nicely regulated Air Conditioner/Condenser and Forced Air Heater that are really great on our energy bill. And I can rest assured that even in an earthquake we won't be at risk with any kind of possible gas leak from our old furnace. Also, the air quality is so much better, and I'm not waking up with a sore throat anymore because of the dry air from our old gas furnace.<//text>

<rating>5< /rating>< Review>
Highly recommend this company to anyone looking for an HONEST and AFFORDABLE heating and/or AC unit! Found on Home Advisor, never thought of calling them because they are an hour's drive from our place. Anna at the office was great about contacting me right away and each and every time I had an appointment with someone from Southland she sent me a reminder. From start to finish, this was an extremely professional job!

Ray was our salesperson and the owner, and our very 1st interview for the job. He set the bar ridiculously high, so after a few other companies came out, it was a no brainer decision to go with Southland.

THe install crew came up during a horrendous rain storm and managed to finish installing a new HVAC system the same day despite the on and off rain. What I love about the workers is that any time they enter your home, they wear booties over their shoes so nothing is tracked in. That has meant a lot with these rainy days.

Southland took care of all the annoying details such as permitting,  scheduling the HERS inspector and final inspection for permit. They even send someone to be there for the final just in case!

Special shout outs to some exceptional employees!! -

John and Benjamin came together for the final permit inspection and were super helpful and polite. I had asked if they would adjust the dampeners in the attic for comfort levels (which was missed in the initial set up) and they worked together to ensure I was happy with each and every register/vent's output. John was even nice enough to confirm my suspicions that our variable speed heater was only working on high. I enjoyed talking with John afterwards as we share a love for the open road and motorbikes.

Jacob had to make a special trip  to fix the variable speed issue. The office made sure I was taken care of as usual, and Jacob spent a good 90 mins checking our NEST thermostat and the wiring of the furnace. He fixed the problem quickly from the NEST, but stuck around to ensure I was comfortable with the way it was running, even showing me how it worked. Again another polite, friendly, no rush, easy to talk to interaction with this Southland employee!

THis wasn't an inexpensive job, but that said SOuthland still had a lower estimate than any other company I would consider doing the job. That combined with the employees who were by far the BEST part of it all, I wouldn't hesitate to recommend this company to anyone!!</Review>

<rating>5</rating><Review>Southland Heating and Air Conditioning exceeded all my expectations!

Justin, the manager who organized the project, sent a team of technicians to my place as scheduled. I was expecting a full-day job but by 2:30 p.m. the new HVAC system was in place and running (the team arrived to my place around 9 a.m.) The team--Willie, Eber and Victor--arrived on location with a new AC system and condenser and started working immediately to prepare for the crane to arrive (I live in a three-story building). Within less than an hour, the crane had arrived as the three gentlemen had unmounted the old systems, both the condenser on the roof and the AC inside my unit's ceiling. Twenty minutes later, the new condenser was on the roof of the building ready to be connected and the old one was down on the street getting ready for recycle (included).

This was a somewhat, complex job. The old HVAC system was about 45 years old and the space to accommodate a new, larger system in the ceiling was challenging (about 5-inches difference). There was supposed to be some drywall cutting planned in the ceiling around the AC's access hatch and fan coil but Eber and the team did some magic and saved the day in every way. They managed to customize the fan space from inside the ceiling and made space for the new unit to fit without having to cut the drywall and create unnecessary work and expenses. All three gentlemen were hard at work, showing professionalism, expertise and courtesy, as they worked between the roof and my unit to complete the project while they made sure my carpet and furniture remain clean (they covered the carpet with tarp and work area with plastic).

The entire team was accommodating. Justin with his quote flexibility and assurances (got multiple discounts) and his prompt replies to my emails (even at 2:00 a.m.), and Willie, Eber and Victor with their work ethics and their desire for a job well done! Thank you gentlemen! Mission accomplished, and job well done! In addition, and to top all that, we had a surprise visit from the co-founder of the company, Dave, to check on the project for quality assurance and quality control. Thanks for stopping by Dave! Dave later contacted me to make sure all work was done and offered an additional discount for a quoted expense that was later determined unneeded during the course of work (Talk about honesty of work). Lest not forget the Accounting team, Ana and Shereen (please forgive me if I misspelled your name), who followed up on the project and made sure that the work was done to my satisfaction.

Thank you Southland Heating and Air Conditioning. You have managed to turn a potential nightmare job into a seamless project. I am forever grateful. Keep up the good work!

Update: A couple of days later, the AC acted up and the thermostat needed configuration. Got in touch again with Justin, who in turn sent Brian to my place as early as the next morning. Awesome Brian checked the unit and determined the source of the problem (something related to voltage distribution to the unit's components). Around an hour later, and a few more heating and cooling tests, a voltage controller was in place and the AC unit was back online.

Thank you guys for your promptness, expertise and efficiency.</Review>< pics>

< Time>
1466613508815< /Time>
<Rating>5<//Rating>< review>
Our home only had one gas wall heater, no duct work. So we needed a completely new HVAC system: furnace, AC, and ductwork. In fall 2015 we'd gotten bids from a few other well-rated companies that were extremely high. All were Lennox dealers. A few months ago I looked into other manufacturers like Trane, and discovered Southland, which had superb reviews on multiple websites. From my first meeting with Matt Alba, I knew the reviews were accurate. Matt was extremely professional, answering all of my questions in a clear, straightforward way, without any gimmicks or high-pressure sales tactics. Their bid was significantly less than the ones we received in the fall. And they were able to install the whole system in one day! Matt was similarly professional in finalizing our plan, scheduling our install date, and helping us coordinate with an electrician to have our electrical panel replaced the same day as the heating and AC install.
The install day went extremely smoothly. Rudy, the site manager, was extremely professional, as was the rest of his crew. They worked very cleanly, covering our floors and furniture with tarps. They were very good at communicating their plans and their progress throughout the day. I found out at the end of the day they were down a couple workers, but were still able to get the job done on time with no hiccups. We've had the system installed for a few days and it works excellently!
I wholeheartedly recommend Southland!<//review>
